<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="schemas"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=schemas">Schemas</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>The base class for all Zod schemas is <code>$ZodType</code>. It accepts two generic parameters: <code>Output</code> and <code>Input</code>.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">export</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> class</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> $ZodType</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&lt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">Output</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> unknown</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">Input</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> unknown</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt; {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">  _zod</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> { </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">/* internals */</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<p><code>zod/v4/core</code> exports a number of subclasses that implement some common parsers. A union of all first-party subclasses is exported as <code>z.$ZodTypes</code>.</p>

<div class="divide-y divide-fd-border overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-card" data-orientation="vertical"><div data-state="closed" data-orientation="vertical" class="group/accordion relative scroll-m-20"><h3 data-orientation="vertical" data-state="closed" class="not-prose flex flex-row items-center text-fd-card-foreground font-medium has-focus-visible:bg-fd-accent"><button type="button" aria-controls="radix-_R_4fiilubv9fl5b_" aria-expanded="false" data-state="closed" data-orientation="vertical" id="radix-_R_fiilubv9fl5b_" class="flex flex-1 items-center gap-2 px-4 py-2.5 text-start focus-visible:outline-none" data-radix-collection-item=""><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-chevron-right -ms-1 size-4 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground transition-transform duration-200 group-data-[state=open]/accordion:rotate-90"><path d="m9 18 6-6-6-6"></path></svg>Inheritance diagram</button></h3><div data-state="closed" id="radix-_R_4fiilubv9fl5b_" hidden="" role="region" aria-labelledby="radix-_R_fiilubv9fl5b_" data-orientation="vertical" class="overflow-hidden data-[state=closed]:animate-fd-accordion-up data-[state=open]:animate-fd-accordion-down" style="--radix-accordion-content-height:var(--radix-collapsible-content-height);--radix-accordion-content-width:var(--radix-collapsible-content-width)"></div></div></div>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="internals"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=internals">Internals</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>All <code>zod/v4/core</code> subclasses only contain a single property: <code>_zod</code>. This property is an object containing the schemas <em>internals</em>. The goal is to make <code>zod/v4/core</code> as extensible and unopinionated as possible. Other libraries can &quot;build their own Zod&quot; on top of these classes without <code>zod/v4/core</code> cluttering up the interface. Refer to the implementations of <code>zod</code> and <code>zod/mini</code> for examples of how to extend these classes.</p>
<p>The <code>_zod</code> internals property contains some notable properties:</p>
<ul>
<li><code>.def</code> — The schema&#x27;s <em>definition</em>: this is the object you pass into the class&#x27;s constructor to create an instance. It completely describes the schema, and it&#x27;s JSON-serializable.<!-- -->
<ul>
<li><code>.def.type</code> — A string representing the schema&#x27;s type, e.g. <code>&quot;string&quot;</code>, <code>&quot;object&quot;</code>, <code>&quot;array&quot;</code>, etc.</li>
<li><code>.def.checks</code> — An array of <em>checks</em> that are executed by the schema after parsing.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>.input</code> — A virtual property that &quot;stores&quot; the schema&#x27;s <em>inferred input type</em>.</li>
<li><code>.output</code> — A virtual property that &quot;stores&quot; the schema&#x27;s <em>inferred output type</em>.</li>
<li><code>.run()</code> — The schema&#x27;s internal parser implementation.</li>
</ul>
<p>If you are implementing a tool (say, a code generator) that must traverse Zod schemas, you can cast any schema to <code>$ZodTypes</code> and use the <code>def</code> property to discriminate between these classes.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">export</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> function</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> walk</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">_schema</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> z</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">$ZodType</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">) {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">  const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> schema</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> _schema </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">as</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> z</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">$ZodTypes</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">  const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> def</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> schema._zod.def;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">  switch</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> (def.type) {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">    case</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;string&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">      // ...</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">      break</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">    case</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;object&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">      // ...</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">      break</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<p>There are a number of subclasses of <code>$ZodString</code> that implement various <em>string formats</em>. These are exported as <code>z.$ZodStringFormatTypes</code>.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" <h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="parsing"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=parsing">Parsing</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>As the Zod Core schema classes have no methods, there are top-level functions for parsing data.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" <h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="checks"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=checks">Checks</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>Every Zod schema contains an array of <em>checks</em>. These perform post-parsing refinements (and occasionally mutations) that <em>do not affect</em> the inferred type.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> schema</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">string</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">().</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">check</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">email</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">()).</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">check</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">min</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">5</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">));</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; $ZodString</span></span>
<span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">schema._zod.def.checks;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; [$ZodCheckEmail, $ZodCheckMinLength]</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<p>The base class for all Zod checks is <code>$ZodCheck</code>. It accepts a single generic parameter <code>T</code>.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">export</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> class</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> $ZodCheck</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&lt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">in</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> T</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> unknown</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt; {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">  _zod</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> { </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">/* internals */</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<p>The <code>_zod</code> internals property contains some notable properties:</p>
<ul>
<li><code>.def</code> — The check&#x27;s <em>definition</em>: this is the object you pass into the class&#x27;s constructor to create the check. It completely describes the check, and it&#x27;s JSON-serializable.<!-- -->
<ul>
<li><code>.def.check</code> — A string representing the check&#x27;s type, e.g. <code>&quot;min_length&quot;</code>, <code>&quot;less_than&quot;</code>, <code>&quot;string_format&quot;</code>, etc.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>.check()</code> — Contains the check&#x27;s validation logic.</li>
</ul>
<p><code>zod/v4/core</code> exports a number of subclasses that perform some common refinements. All first-party subclasses are exported as a union called <code>z.$ZodChecks</code>.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide <p>You can use the <code>._zod.def.check</code> property to discriminate between these classes.</p>

<p>As with schema types, there are a number of subclasses of <code>$ZodCheckStringFormat</code> that implement various <em>string formats</em>.</p>

<p>Use a nested <code>switch</code> to discriminate between the different string format checks.</p>

<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">      const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> formatCheck</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> check </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">as</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> z</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">$ZodStringFormatChecks</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">      const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> formatCheckDef</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> formatCheck._zod.def;</span></span>
<span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">      switch</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> (formatCheckDef.format) {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">        case</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;email&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">        case</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;url&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">          // do stuff</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">      }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">    break</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<p>You&#x27;ll notice some of these string format <em>checks</em> overlap with the string format <em>types</em> above. That&#x27;s because these classes implement both the <code>$ZodCheck</code> and <code>$ZodType</code> interfaces. That is, they can be used as either a check or a type. In these cases, both <code>._zod.parse</code> (the schema parser) and <code>._zod.check</code> (the check validation) are executed during parsing. In effect, the instance is prepended to its own <code>checks</code> array (though it won&#x27;t actually exist in <code>._zod.def.checks</code>).</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// as a type</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">email</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">().</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">parse</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;<a href="/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection" class="__cf_email__" data-cfemail="1c696f796e5c79647d716c7079327f7371">[email&#160;protected]</a>&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">);</span></span>
<span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// as a check</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">string</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">().</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">check</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">email</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">()).</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">parse</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;<a href="/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection" class="__cf_email__" data-cfemail="99eceafcebd9fce1f8f4e9f5fcb7faf6f4">[email&#160;protected]</a>&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="errors"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=errors">Errors</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>The base class for all errors in Zod is <code>$ZodError</code>.</p>
<div class="my-6 flex flex-row gap-2 rounded-lg border border-s-2 bg-fd-card p-3 text-sm text-fd-card-foreground shadow-md border-s-blue-500/50"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-info size-5 fill-blue-500 text-fd-card"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"></circle><path d="M12 16v-4"></path><path d="M12 8h.01"></path></svg><div class="min-w-0 flex-1"><div class="text-fd-muted-foreground prose-no-margin">
<p>For performance reasons, <code>$ZodError</code> <em>does not</em> extend the built-in <code>Error</code> class! So using <code>instanceof Error</code> will return <code>false</code>.</p>
</div></div></div>
<ul>
<li>The <code>zod</code> package implements a subclass of <code>$ZodError</code> called <code>ZodError</code> with some additional convenience methods.</li>
<li>The <code>zod/mini</code> sub-package directly uses <code>$ZodError</code></li>
</ul>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">export</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> class</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> $ZodError</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&lt;</span><span unknown</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt; </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">implements</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> Error</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> public</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70"> issues</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> $ZodIssue</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">[];</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="issues"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=issues">Issues</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>The <code>issues</code> property corresponds to an array of <code>$ZodIssue</code> objects. All issues extend the <code>z.$ZodIssueBase</code> interface.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 <span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">  readonly</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70"> code</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">?:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> string</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">  readonly</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70"> input</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">?:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> unknown</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">  readonly</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70"> path</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> PropertyKey</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">[];</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">  readonly</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70"> message</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> string</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<p>Zod defines the following issue subtypes:</p>

<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">  |</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> $ZodIssueInvalidValue</span></span>

<p>For details on each type, refer to <a href="https://github.com/colinhacks/zod/blob/main/packages/zod/src/v4/core/errors.ts" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">the implementation</a>.</p>

Zod Core\n\nimport { Callout } from \"fumadocs-ui/components/callout\"\nimport { Accordion, Accordions } from 'fumadocs-ui/components/accordion';\n\nThis sub-package exports the core classes and utilities that are consumed by Zod and Zod Mini. It is not intended to be used directly; instead it's designed to be extended by other packages. It implements:\n\n```ts\nimport * as z from \"zod/v4/core\";\n\n// the base class for all Zod schemas\nz.$ZodType;\n\n// subclasses of $ZodType that implement common parsers\nz.$ZodString\nz.$ZodObject\nz.$ZodArray\n// ...\n\n// the base class for all Zod checks\nz.$ZodCheck;\n\n// subclasses of $ZodCheck that implement common checks\nz.$ZodCheckMinLength\nz.$ZodCheckMaxLength\n\n// the base class for all Zod errors\nz.$ZodError;\n\n// issue formats (types only)\n{} as z.$ZodIssue;\n\n// utils\nz.util.isValidJWT(...);\n```\n\n## Schemas\n\nThe base class for all Zod schemas is `$ZodType`. It accepts two generic parameters: `Output` and `Input`.\n\n```ts\nexport class $ZodType\u003cOutput = unknown, Input = unknown\u003e {\n  _zod: { /* internals */}\n}\n```\n\n`zod/v4/core` exports a number of subclasses that implement some common parsers. A union of all first-party subclasses is exported as `z.$ZodTypes`.\n\n```ts\nexport type $ZodTypes =\n  | $ZodString\n  | $ZodNumber\n  | $ZodBigInt\n  | $ZodBoolean\n  | $ZodDate\n  | $ZodSymbol\n  | $ZodUndefined\n  | $ZodNullable\n  | $ZodNull\n  | $ZodAny\n  | $ZodUnknown\n  | $ZodNever\n  | $ZodVoid\n  | $ZodArray\n  | $ZodObject\n  | $ZodUnion // $ZodDiscriminatedUnion extends this\n  | $ZodIntersection\n  | $ZodTuple\n  | $ZodRecord\n  | $ZodMap\n  | $ZodSet\n  | $ZodLiteral\n  | $ZodEnum\n  | $ZodPromise\n  | $ZodLazy\n  | $ZodOptional\n  | $ZodDefault\n  | $ZodTemplateLiteral\n  | $ZodCustom\n  | $ZodTransform\n  | $ZodNonOptional\n  | $ZodReadonly\n  | $ZodNaN\n  | $ZodPipe // $ZodCodec extends this\n  | $ZodSuccess\n  | $ZodCatch\n  | $ZodFile;\n```\n\n\u003cAccordions\u003e\n  \u003cAccordion title=\"Inheritance diagram\"\u003e\n    Here is a complete inheritance diagram for the core schema classes:\n\n    ```txt\n    - $ZodType\n        - $ZodString\n            - $ZodStringFormat\n                - $ZodGUID\n                - $ZodUUID\n                - $ZodEmail\n                - $ZodURL\n                - $ZodEmoji\n                - $ZodNanoID\n                - $ZodCUID\n                - $ZodCUID2\n                - $ZodULID\n                - $ZodXID\n                - $ZodKSUID\n                - $ZodISODateTime\n                - $ZodISODate\n                - $ZodISOTime\n                - $ZodISODuration\n                - $ZodIPv4\n                - $ZodIPv6\n                - $ZodCIDRv4\n                - $ZodCIDRv6\n                - $ZodBase64\n                - $ZodBase64URL\n                - $ZodE164\n                - $ZodJWT\n        - $ZodNumber\n            - $ZodNumberFormat\n        - $ZodBigInt\n            - $ZodBigIntFormat\n        - $ZodBoolean\n        - $ZodSymbol\n        - $ZodUndefined\n        - $ZodNull\n        - $ZodAny\n        - $ZodUnknown\n        - $ZodNever\n        - $ZodVoid\n        - $ZodDate\n        - $ZodArray\n        - $ZodObject\n        - $ZodUnion\n            - $ZodDiscriminatedUnion\n        - $ZodIntersection\n        - $ZodTuple\n        - $ZodRecord\n        - $ZodMap\n        - $ZodSet\n        - $ZodEnum\n        - $ZodLiteral\n        - $ZodFile\n        - $ZodTransform\n        - $ZodOptional\n        - $ZodNullable\n        - $ZodDefault\n        - $ZodPrefault\n        - $ZodNonOptional\n        - $ZodSuccess\n        - $ZodCatch\n        - $ZodNaN\n        - $ZodPipe\n            - $ZodCodec\n        - $ZodReadonly\n        - $ZodTemplateLiteral\n        - $ZodCustom\n\n    ```\n  \u003c/Accordion\u003e\n\u003c/Accordions\u003e\n\n## Internals\n\nAll `zod/v4/core` subclasses only contain a single property: `_zod`. This property is an object containing the schemas *internals*. The goal is to make `zod/v4/core` as extensible and unopinionated as possible. Other libraries can \"build their own Zod\" on top of these classes without `zod/v4/core` cluttering up the interface. Refer to the implementations of `zod` and `zod/mini` for examples of how to extend these classes.\n\nThe `_zod` internals property contains some notable properties:\n\n* `.def` — The schema's *definition*: this is the object you pass into the class's constructor to create an instance. It completely describes the schema, and it's JSON-serializable.\n  * `.def.type` — A string representing the schema's type, e.g. `\"string\"`, `\"object\"`, `\"array\"`, etc.\n  * `.def.checks` — An array of *checks* that are executed by the schema after parsing.\n* `.input` — A virtual property that \"stores\" the schema's *inferred input type*.\n* `.output` — A virtual property that \"stores\" the schema's *inferred output type*.\n* `.run()` — The schema's internal parser implementation.\n\nIf you are implementing a tool (say, a code generator) that must traverse Zod schemas, you can cast any schema to `$ZodTypes` and use the `def` property to discriminate between these classes.\n\n```ts\nexport function walk(_schema: z.$ZodType) {\n  const schema = _schema as z.$ZodTypes;\n  const def = schema._zod.def;\n  switch (def.type) {\n    case \"string\": {\n      // ...\n      break;\n    }\n    case \"object\": {\n      // ...\n      break;\n    }\n  }\n}\n```\n\nThere are a number of subclasses of `$ZodString` that implement various *string formats*. These are exported as `z.$ZodStringFormatTypes`.\n\n```ts\nexport type $ZodStringFormatTypes =\n  | $ZodGUID\n  | $ZodUUID\n  | $ZodEmail\n  | $ZodURL\n  | $ZodEmoji\n  | $ZodNanoID\n  | $ZodCUID\n  | $ZodCUID2\n  | $ZodULID\n  | $ZodXID\n  | $ZodKSUID\n  | $ZodISODateTime\n  | $ZodISODate\n  | $ZodISOTime\n  | $ZodISODuration\n  | $ZodIPv4\n  | $ZodIPv6\n  | $ZodCIDRv4\n  | $ZodCIDRv6\n  | $ZodBase64\n  | $ZodBase64URL\n  | $ZodE164\n  | $ZodJWT\n```\n\n## Parsing\n\nAs the Zod Core schema classes have no methods, there are top-level functions for parsing data.\n\n```ts\nimport * as z from \"zod/v4/core\";\n\nconst schema = new z.$ZodString({ type: \"string\" });\nz.parse(schema, \"hello\");\nz.safeParse(schema, \"hello\");\nawait z.parseAsync(schema, \"hello\");\nawait z.safeParseAsync(schema, \"hello\");\n```\n\n## Checks\n\nEvery Zod schema contains an array of *checks*. These perform post-parsing refinements (and occasionally mutations) that *do not affect* the inferred type.\n\n```ts\nconst schema = z.string().check(z.email()).check(z.min(5));\n// =\u003e $ZodString\n\nschema._zod.def.checks;\n// =\u003e [$ZodCheckEmail, $ZodCheckMinLength]\n```\n\nThe base class for all Zod checks is `$ZodCheck`. It accepts a single generic parameter `T`.\n\n```ts\nexport class $ZodCheck\u003cin T = unknown\u003e {\n  _zod: { /* internals */}\n}\n```\n\nThe `_zod` internals property contains some notable properties:\n\n* `.def` — The check's *definition*: this is the object you pass into the class's constructor to create the check. It completely describes the check, and it's JSON-serializable.\n  * `.def.check` — A string representing the check's type, e.g. `\"min_length\"`, `\"less_than\"`, `\"string_format\"`, etc.\n* `.check()` — Contains the check's validation logic.\n\n`zod/v4/core` exports a number of subclasses that perform some common refinements. All first-party subclasses are exported as a union called `z.$ZodChecks`.\n\n```ts\nexport type $ZodChecks =\n  | $ZodCheckLessThan\n  | $ZodCheckGreaterThan\n  | $ZodCheckMultipleOf\n  | $ZodCheckNumberFormat\n  | $ZodCheckBigIntFormat\n  | $ZodCheckMaxSize\n  | $ZodCheckMinSize\n  | $ZodCheckSizeEquals\n  | $ZodCheckMaxLength\n  | $ZodCheckMinLength\n  | $ZodCheckLengthEquals\n  | $ZodCheckProperty\n  | $ZodCheckMimeType\n  | $ZodCheckOverwrite\n  | $ZodCheckStringFormat\n```\n\nYou can use the `._zod.def.check` property to discriminate between these classes.\n\n```ts\nconst check = {} as z.$ZodChecks;\nconst def = check._zod.def;\n\nswitch (def.check) {\n  case \"less_than\":\n  case \"greater_than\":\n    // ...\n    break;\n}\n```\n\nAs with schema types, there are a number of subclasses of `$ZodCheckStringFormat` that implement various *string formats*.\n\n```ts\nexport type $ZodStringFormatChecks =\n  | $ZodCheckRegex\n  | $ZodCheckLowerCase\n  | $ZodCheckUpperCase\n  | $ZodCheckIncludes\n  | $ZodCheckStartsWith\n  | $ZodCheckEndsWith\n  | $ZodGUID\n  | $ZodUUID\n  | $ZodEmail\n  | $ZodURL\n  | $ZodEmoji\n  | $ZodNanoID\n  | $ZodCUID\n  | $ZodCUID2\n  | $ZodULID\n  | $ZodXID\n  | $ZodKSUID\n  | $ZodISODateTime\n  | $ZodISODate\n  | $ZodISOTime\n  | $ZodISODuration\n  | $ZodIPv4\n  | $ZodIPv6\n  | $ZodCIDRv4\n  | $ZodCIDRv6\n  | $ZodBase64\n  | $ZodBase64URL\n  | $ZodE164\n  | $ZodJWT;\n```\n\nUse a nested `switch` to discriminate between the different string format checks.\n\n```ts\nconst check = {} as z.$ZodChecks;\nconst def = check._zod.def;\n\nswitch (def.check) {\n  case \"less_than\":\n  case \"greater_than\":\n  // ...\n  case \"string_format\":\n    {\n      const formatCheck = check as z.$ZodStringFormatChecks;\n      const formatCheckDef = formatCheck._zod.def;\n\n      switch (formatCheckDef.format) {\n        case \"email\":\n        case \"url\":\n          // do stuff\n      }\n    }\n    break;\n}\n```\n\nYou'll notice some of these string format *checks* overlap with the string format *types* above. That's because these classes implement both the `$ZodCheck` and `$ZodType` interfaces. That is, they can be used as either a check or a type. In these cases, both `._zod.parse` (the schema parser) and `._zod.check` (the check validation) are executed during parsing. In effect, the instance is prepended to its own `checks` array (though it won't actually exist in `._zod.def.checks`).\n\n```ts\n// as a type\nz.email().parse(\"user@example.com\");\n\n// as a check\nz.string().check(z.email()).parse(\"user@example.com\")\n```\n\n## Errors\n\nThe base class for all errors in Zod is `$ZodError`.\n\n\u003e For performance reasons, `$ZodError` *does not* extend the built-in `Error` class! So using `instanceof Error` will return `false`.\n\n* The `zod` package implements a subclass of `$ZodError` called `ZodError` with some additional convenience methods.\n* The `zod/mini` sub-package directly uses `$ZodError`\n\n```ts\nexport class $ZodError\u003cT = unknown\u003e implements Error {\n public issues: $ZodIssue[];\n}\n```\n\n## Issues\n\nThe `issues` property corresponds to an array of `$ZodIssue` objects. All issues extend the `z.$ZodIssueBase` interface.\n\n```ts\nexport interface $ZodIssueBase {\n  readonly code?: string;\n  readonly input?: unknown;\n  readonly path: PropertyKey[];\n  readonly message: string;\n}\n```\n\nZod defines the following issue subtypes:\n\n```ts\nexport type $ZodIssue =\n  | $ZodIssueInvalidType\n  | $ZodIssueTooBig\n  | $ZodIssueTooSmall\n  | $ZodIssueInvalidStringFormat\n  | $ZodIssueNotMultipleOf\n  | $ZodIssueUnrecognizedKeys\n  | $ZodIssueInvalidUnion\n  | $ZodIssueInvalidKey\n  | $ZodIssueInvalidElement\n  | $ZodIssueInvalidValue\n  | $ZodIssueCustom;\n```\n\nFor details on each type, refer to [the implementation](https://github.com/colinhacks/zod/blob/main/packages/zod/src/v4/core/errors.ts).\n\n{/* ## Best practices\n\n  If you're reading this page, you're likely trying to build some kind of tool or library on top of Zod. This section breaks down some best practices for doing so.\n\n  1. If you're just accept user-defined schemas, use Standard Schema instead\n\n  Zod implements the [Standard Schema](https://standardschema.dev/) specification, a standard interface for schema libraries to expose their validation logic and inferred types to third-party tools. If your goal is to accept user-defined schemas, extracting their inferred types, and using them to parse data, then Standard Schema is all you need. Refer to the Standard Schema website/docs for more information.\n\n  2. Set up `peerDependencies` properly!\n\n  If your tool accepts Zod schemas from a consumer/user, you should add `\"zod/v4/core\"` to `peerDependencies`. This lets your users \"bring their own Zod\". Be as flexible as possible with the version range. For example, if your tool is compatible with `zod/v4/core`, you can use the following. This allows your users to bring any version of `zod/v4/core`, avoiding accidental duplicate installs.\n\n\n  ```json\n  {\n  \"peerDependencies\": {\n    \"zod/v4/core\": \"*\"\n  }\n  }\n  ```\n\n  Since package managers generally won't install your own `peerDependencies`, you'll need to add `zod/v4/core` to your `devDependencies` as well. As new versions of `zod/v4/core` are released, you can update your `devDependencies` to match the latest version. This is important for testing and development purposes.\n\n  ```json\n  {\n  \"peerDependencies\": {\n    \"zod\": \"*\"\n  },\n  \"devDependencies\": {\n    \"zod\": \"^3.25.0\"\n  }\n  }\n  ``` */}\n"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"26:[\"$\",\"$L32\",null,{\"toc\":[{\"depth\":2,\"url\":\"#schemas\",\"title\":\"Schemas\"},{\"depth\":2,\"url\":\"#internals\",\"title\":\"Internals\"},{\"depth\":2,\"url\":\"#parsing\",\"title\":\"Parsing\"},{\"depth\":2,\"url\":\"#checks\",\"title\":\"Checks\"},{\"depth\":2,\"url\":\"#errors\",\"title\":\"Errors\"},{\"depth\":2,\"url\":\"#issues\",\"title\":\"Issues\"}],\"single\":false,\"children\":[[\"$\",\"$L33\",null,{\"className\":\"\",\"style\":{\"--fd-tocnav-height\":\"$undefined\"},\"children\":[[\"$\",\"$L34\",null,{\"className\":\"h-10\",\"children\":[[\"$\",\"$L35\",null,{\"className\":\"w-full\",\"items\":\"$26:props:toc\"}],[\"$\",\"$L36\",null,{\"children\":[\"$undefined\",[\"$\",\"$L37\",null,{\"isMenu\":true,\"children\":[\"$\",\"$L38\",null,{\"items\":\"$26:props:toc\"}]}],\"$undefined\"]}]]}],[\"$\",\"$L39\",null,{\"className\":\"max-w-[860px]\",\"children\":[[\"$\",\"$L3a\",null,{}],[[\"$\",\"div\",null,{\"className\":\"mb-6\",\"children\":[[\"$\",\"h1\",null,{\"ref\":\"$undefined\",\"children\":\"Zod
